<plain_text><page sequence="1">Subject Index Persons named in entries with review suffixes (ra, rb, rv) are authors, editors, performers, directors, artists, or persons otherwise involved in the creation of the items treated in the reviews. Parenthetical notes after names of persons indicate the description of their role on the title page, cover, or in the byline of the item reviewed, or the indexer's inference regarding that role. Persons named in entries without review suffixes are named or discussed in the items. Lower-case words set off with quotation marks (e.g., folklore) indicate items that focus on definition. JAF items with spellings that varied in minor ways over the past century are generally grouped under the moder spelling: the entryfolklore in this list includes words spelled in Journal articles, reviews, notes, and announcements as folk-lore, folklore, and folk lore.
